
---
# 3.0 Plot Jaccard Distance between clusters
---

Low jaccard distance means markers genes for clusters are very similar.


```R
#most common marker genes
#sort(table(dat$Gene),decreasing=TRUE)[1:200]
```


```R
#create binary matrix of marker genes across clusters
b <- table(dat$Gene, dat$Cluster)
b <- as.matrix(b)
b[1:5, 1:5]
```



               BT127_L_C1 BT127_L_C2 BT147_L_C1 BT147_L_C2 BT48_L_C1
      A1BG              0          0          0          0         0
      A1BG-AS1          0          0          0          0         0
      A2M               1          0          0          0         0
      A4GALT            0          0          0          0         0
      AAAS              0          0          1          0         1



```R
#compute the overlap (similarity) of marker gene profiles for each cluster
#use the bianry distance in R, which is the same as computing the jaccard distance
#Jaccaard distance measures dissimilairty between sample sets, subtracting Jaccard coefficient from 1
# Jaccard distance = 1-(jaccard coefficient)

jaccard <- dist(t(b), method = "binary")
str(jaccard)
```

    Class 'dist'  atomic [1:3655] 1 0.898 0.948 0.933 0.911 ...
      ..- attr(*, "Size")= int 86
      ..- attr(*, "Labels")= chr [1:86] "BT127_L_C1" "BT127_L_C2" "BT147_L_C1" "BT147_L_C2" ...
      ..- attr(*, "Diag")= logi FALSE
      ..- attr(*, "Upper")= logi FALSE
      ..- attr(*, "method")= chr "binary"
      ..- attr(*, "call")= language dist(x = t(b), method = "binary")



```R
hc <- hclust(jaccard, method = "complete")
```


```R
#pdf("~/Desktop/IntraClusterDendrogram.pdf")
plot(hc, hang = -1, cex = 0.4)
#dev.off()
```


![png](output_5_0.png)



```R
##convert jaccard distance to jaccard index

jaccard_index <- 1-as.matrix(jaccard)
#head(jaccard_index)
```


```R
magma(n=15, direction = -1)
?magma
```

```R
#pdf("~/Desktop/Cluster_BinaryDist.pdf", width = 6, height = 6)


col_fun = colorRamp2(c(0,1), c("white", "blue"))
Heatmap(as.matrix(jaccard_index),
        name = "Jaccard \nIndex",
        col = c("white", magma(n=15, direction = -1)),
        row_names_gp = gpar(fontsize = 4),
        column_names_gp = gpar(fontsize = 4),
        column_split = 2,
        row_split = 2

       )

#dev.off()
```

### Calculate mean jaccard index of all the similar clusters


```R
sim.clust <- c("G885_L_C1",
"G566_L_C2",
"BT89_L_C1" ,
"BT147_L_C1" ,
"BT67_L_C1" ,
"G620_L_C3" ,
"G637_L_C3" ,
"G946.K_L_C2",
"G876_L_C2" ,
"G800_L_C2" ,
"G799_L_C3" ,
"G797_L_C3" ,
"G620_L_C5" ,
"BT84_L_C2"
)
```


```R
colnames(jaccard_index) <- gsub("-", ".", colnames(jaccard_index))
rownames(jaccard_index) <- gsub("-", ".", rownames(jaccard_index))
```


```R
df <- data.frame(as.matrix(jaccard_index))

gg <- df[rownames(df) %in% sim.clust, colnames(df) %in% sim.clust]
gg
dim(gg)
```

```R
indices <- unlist(gg, use.names = F)
indices <- indices[!indices == 1] #remove all the 1s from same sample to same sample correlation
indices
mean(indices)
```

## calculate mean and range of remaining clusters
----


```R
df <- data.frame(as.matrix(jaccard_index))

gg <- df[!rownames(df) %in% sim.clust, !colnames(df) %in% sim.clust]
gg
dim(gg)
```

```R
"G637_L_C3" ,
"G946−K_L_C2",
"G876_L_C2" ,
"G800_L_C2" ,
"G799_L_C3" ,
"G797_L_C3" ,
"G620_L_C5" ,
"BT84_L_C2"
               )
length(sim.clust)

a <- dat[dat$Cluster %in% sim.clust, ]
dim(a)
b <- dat[dat$Cluster == 'G946-K_L_C2', ] #for some reason this will not pull out of data frame
dim(b)

all.genes <- c(b$Gene, a$Gene)
length(all.genes)

genes <- names(table(all.genes)[(table(all.genes) >= 14)]) #list of genes shared by all 14 clusters
length(genes)

#358 genes found in all clusters

genes
write.table(genes, file = "~/Desktop/CommonMarkers_14clusters_BTSC_Sept2019.txt",
            quote = F,
            row.names = F,
            col.names = F
           )
```

 ----
#### Findings

Across 29 samples, a set of clusters from  14 clusters from 13 samples have high marker similarity. They share 358 common marker genes found in all 14 clusters are related to cell cycling, expression of the DREAM complex nd oligodendrocyte differentiation (MSigDB) pathway analysis.


Is this really interesting enough to put in the paper.....?

---

```R
##subset to top 20 pathways
dat$log10.padj <- -log10(dat$p.adjust)
dat$ID <- factor(dat$ID, levels = rev(dat$ID))
```

```R
p <- ggplot(data=dat, aes(x=ID, y=Count, fill = log10.padj)) +
    geom_bar(stat="identity") +
    coord_flip() + xlab ("") + ylab("Gene Count") +
     scale_fill_gradient(low="blue", high="red", name = "Enrichment\n-log10(p.adjust)") + ggtitle("GSC Proliferation Module (358 genes)") + theme_classic() +
    theme(axis.text.x = element_text(angle = 0, hjust = 1)) +
      theme(panel.border = element_rect
            (linetype = "solid", fill = NA)) + theme(text = element_text(size=13))

pdf("~/Desktop/GSC_clustercommonMarkers.pdf", width =11, height = 5)
p
dev.off()
```

## 6.0 Plot a heatmap (or DotPlot) of example marker genes in specific examples
---

This will be for the main figure of Figure 2 panel A.   
Plot expression of select marker genes from cluster averaged scaled data.   

Analysis Dir: /mnt/work1/users/pughlab/projects/BTSCs_scRNAseq/Manuscript_G607removed/CommonMarkerGenes_BTSCs


```R
suppressMessages(library("Seurat", lib ="/mnt/work1/users/pughlab/projects/BTSCs_scRNAseq/Manuscript/lib/" ))

#load in all BTSC data
load("/mnt/work1/users/pughlab/projects/BTSCs_scRNAseq/Manuscript_G607removed/data/SeuratObj/BTSCs/Global_SU2C_BTSCs_CCregressed_noRibo.Rdata")
str(BTSC)

#make sure identity is intra BTSC cluster
BTSC <- SetIdent(BTSC, ident.use = factor(BTSC@meta.data$IntraBTSC.ID))

#
pdf("Dotplot_BTSC_86cluster_MarkerGenes.pdf", height = 25, width = 5)

DotPlot(BTSC, genes.plot = c("MKI67", "TOP2A", "ARHGAP11A", "BRCA1", "HMGB2"),
        dot.scale = 4,
        plot.legend = T,
        cols.use = c("blue", "white", "red")

       )

dev.off()

```


```R
## make a heatmap on cluster averages

cluster.averages <- AverageExpression(BTSC,
                                      return.seurat = TRUE

                                    )
genes <- c("MKI67",
           "TOP2A",
           "ARHGAP11A",
           "ARHGAP11B",
           "BRCA1",
           "HMGB2",
           "SOX10",
           "EGFR",
           "CD44",
           "CD24",
           "STMN1"
          )

pdf("Dotplot_BTSC_86cluster_MarkerGenes.pdf", width = 30)
DoHeatmap(cluster.averages,
          genes.use = genes,
          group.label.rot = TRUE,
          group.cex = 0
         )
dev.off()

save(cluster.averages, file = "BTSC_intraClusterAverages.Rdata")
```

Subject MM11 exhibited two transcriptional states, both expressing high levels of CCND1 and FRZB; one state was characterized by significant overexpression of endothelial differentiation related factor 1 (EDF1), involved in lipid metabolism and the PPARγ pathway35,36, while the second transcrip- tional clonotype overexpresses PCBD1, a transcriptional co-activator of HNF137.

```R
sample <- "G837_L"
markers <-


load.file <- list.files(pattern = "RData")[grep(sample, list.files(pattern = "RData"))]
load.file
load(load.file)

BTSC <- SetIdent(BTSC, ident.use = factor(BTSC@meta.data$Cluster.ID))

file.name <- paste0("~/Desktop/", sample, "_markerHeatmap.pdf")
pdf(file.name, width = 8, height = 2)

DoHeatmap(BTSC,
          genes.use = markers,
          group.label.rot = TRUE,
          group.cex = 0,
          cex.col = 0,
          title = paste0(sample, ": ", ncol(BTSC@data), " cells")
         )

dev.off()
```

```R
samples <- gsub('.{3}$', '', sim.clust)
samples <- gsub(".K", "-K", samples)
samples <- unique(samples)

cells <- colnames(cluster.averages@data)[gsub('.{3}$', '', colnames(cluster.averages@data)) %in% samples]
cells

dat <- data.matrix(cluster.averages@data)[markers, cells]
head(dat)
```

```R
intrasample_z <- list()
breaks <- c()

for(i in 1:length(samples)){

sample <- samples[i]
print(sample)


subset <- dat[, grep(samples[i], colnames(dat))]
breaks[i] <- length(grep(samples[i], colnames(dat)))
subset <- scale(t(subset))

intrasample_z[[sample]] <- subset

    }

intrasample_z <- t(do.call(rbind, intrasample_z))
```

## 9.0 Plot proliferation across all patients

```R
library(Seurat)
library(pheatmap)

load("~/Desktop/Samwise/projects/BTSCs_scRNAseq/Manuscript_G607removed/CommonMarkerGenes_BTSCs/BTSC_intraClusterAverages.Rdata")

markers <- c("MKI67", "TOP2A", "AURKA", "ARHGAP11A", "ARHGAP11B", "BRCA1", "HMGB2", "CDC45")


samples <- samples <- gsub('.{3}$', '', colnames(cluster.averages@data))
samples

dat <- data.matrix(cluster.averages@data)[markers, ]
head(dat)

#dat[dat > 2.5] <- 2.5
#dat[dat < -2.5] <- -2.5


intrasample_z <- list()

for(i in 1:length(samples)){


sample <- samples[i]
print(sample)


subset <- dat[, grep(sample, colnames(dat))]
head(subset)
subset <- scale(t(subset))
head(subset)

intrasample_z[[sample]] <- subset

    }

intrasample_z <- do.call(rbind, intrasample_z)

```

